e1000\+\_\+rxpbs\+\_\+adjust\+\_\+82580 -\/ adjust R\+X\+P\+BS value to reflect actual Rx P\+BA size \+: data received by reading R\+X\+P\+BS register

3292             \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} fail;
3293 
3294         status = \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_ac9355591fd2dcd37da2fbdf0122b3506}{e1000\_clock\_out\_i2c\_byte}(hw, data);
3295         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (status != \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_ade686b442ce8b2b1dede6968fec28c10}{E1000\_SUCCESS})
3296             \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} fail;
3297 
3298         status = \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a31066319a89802c1be6c7b9542b84010}{e1000\_get\_i2c\_ack}(hw);
3299         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (status != \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__defines_8h_ade686b442ce8b2b1dede6968fec28c10}{E1000\_SUCCESS})
3300             \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} fail;
3301 
3302         \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a22d83c91b88e0f2c27e4aa5d26b280fd}{e1000\_i2c\_stop}(hw);
3303         \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
3304 
3305 fail:
3306         \hyperlink{e1000__82575_8c_a28776e3addb8872f45bb8c11cfa55701}{e1000\_i2c\_bus\_clear}(hw);
3307         retry++;
3308         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (retry < max\_retry)
3309             \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a3732dd7571f0d578b722df9d5a6e8c9a}{DEBUGOUT}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"I2C byte write error - Retrying.\(\backslash\)n"});
3310         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
3311             \hyperlink{kmod_2igb_2e1000__osdep_8h_a3732dd7571f0d578b722df9d5a6e8c9a}{DEBUGOUT}(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"I2C byte write error.\(\backslash\)n"});
3312     \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (retry < max\_retry);
3313 
3314     hw->\hyperlink{structe1000__hw_aab7fce7aa13ba97459b3b65acf02f520}{mac}.\hyperlink{structe1000__mac__info_a6ac57b9c85404edae44f08fe43d7ff02}{ops}.\hyperlink{structe1000__mac__operations_a0aa9b26ec01a96e7f41f49e00f527ae3}{release\_swfw\_sync}(hw, swfw\_mask);
3315 
3316 write\_byte\_out:
3317 
3318     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} status;
3319 \}
\end{DoxyCode}
